[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer heap-buffer-overflow was detected in libxml2’s XML parser when [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing a fuzzed input. The overflow occurs in the function [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:777[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during entity expansion, leading to a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmulti-byte read beyond the bounds of a heap buffer and causing the process to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mabort.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing with libFuzzer, AddressSanitizer reports a [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow in `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure`. The sanitizer log shows a [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m-byte[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread past the end of a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte heap allocation. The crash is reproducible with a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecific testcase provided to the fuzzer harness.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a heap‐based buffer overflow in the XML parser’s entity handling logic.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow is detected by `__asan_memcpy` while copying data in [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlSBufAddEntitySecure`.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The offending buffer was allocated via `xmlStrdup` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlstring.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m through the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing allocator `xmlFuzzMalloc`.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The call stack traces through:  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:777[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue` → `xmlParseEntityValue` → `xmlParseEntityDecl` → [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseInternalSubset` → `xmlParseDocument` → `xmlCtxtParseDocument`  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – The fuzzer entry point `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `fuzz/xml.c`.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • ASan shadow memory indicates the read occurs immediately after the end of the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated region, confirming an out‐of‐bounds access.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer was invoked with flags: `-[0m[33mrss_limit_mb[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m2560[0m[39m -[0m[33mtimeout[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m25[0m[39m -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m … [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-[0m[33mdict[0m[39m=[0m[35mxml[0m[39m.dict`.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To understand the full context of this overflow, the following components should [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe reviewed:  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • parser.c – especially `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure`, `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseEntityValue`, `xmlParseEntityDecl`, `xmlParseInternalSubset`, and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlCtxtParseDocument`.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • xmlstring.c – the implementations of `xmlStrdup` and `xmlStrndup`.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • entities.c and SAX2.c – functions such as `xmlCreateEntity`, `xmlAddEntity`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `xmlSAX2EntityDecl` that build and register entities.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzing harness in `fuzz/xml.c`, which drives parsing under libFuzzer.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Any related buffer‐management logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mallocation sizes, length calculations[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe parser and supporting modules.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Ensure that the buffer is double the necessary size[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The patch replaces this with:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap - buf->size < len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Ensure that the buffer has enough capacity to hold the new data[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->mem + buf->size, str, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- After rebuilding and re-running the same fuzz testcase under ASan, the same [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow is reported at the same `memcpy` site in [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:777[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The error trace, allocation size, and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mredzone details remain effectively unchanged from the initial run.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for further investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The logic in `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` concerning how `len` is computed versus how[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmuch space remains in `buf->mem`.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The behavior and implementation of `xmlSBufGrow`, especially whether it actually [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpands capacity adequately when invoked with `len` rather than a larger [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiplier.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- How the parser constructs and passes entity value strings into [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlSBufAddEntitySecure`, including any pre-calculated or assumed buffer sizes in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe calls from `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue` and related functions.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The memory allocation path starting from `xmlFuzzMalloc` through `xmlStrndup`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlCreateEntity`, and `xmlAddEntity`, to understand the initial buffer capacities [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand potential off-by-one or size-underestimation issues.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The broader parsing flow in `xmlParseEntityDecl` and `xmlParseInternalSubset` for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many assumptions about entity value lengths or nested entity expansions that could [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbypass correct buffer sizing.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The crash happens when xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue reads or copies [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes past [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe end of a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte allocated region.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The buffer in question is managed by xmlSBuf [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma parser string buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow emerges during processing of parameter entity values within [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlParseEntityValue → xmlParseEntityDecl → xmlParseInternalSubset → [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlParseDocument.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The minimal stack at the crash site shows __asan_memcpy called from [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure, indicating insufficient xmlSBufGrow capacity.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In xmlSBufAddEntitySecure [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m766[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the original guard `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap == [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and doubling strategy was replaced with a check `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap - buf->size < [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlen[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, growing the buffer by exactly `len`.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m4000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the patch removed a prior [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlSBufGrow with `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr - chunk[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and instead grows by the combined size of the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchunk delta plus `ent->length`, then adds the entity data and updates `chunk = [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstr`.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLog After Patch  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer run reproduces the overflow at the same address [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x5020[0m[39m…b37[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, same [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m-byte region, same call stack, now attributed to parser.[0m[1;92mc:776[0m[39m after patch.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The allocator stack trace remains unchanged, showing xmlFuzzMalloc → xmlStrndup →[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlCreateEntity.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Shadow bytes and ASan summary confirm a heap left redzone violation.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The xmlSBuf structure and its cap/size invariants: verify initial allocation [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize, capacity updates, and redzone margins.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All xmlSBufGrow calls: ensure they account for both existing data and any future [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minserts [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding multi-stage expansions[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue logic: examine loop bounds, pointer arithmetic on [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`chunk` and `str`, and how partial entity expansions accumulate in the buffer.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Interactions between xmlParseEntityValue, xmlParseEntityDecl, and entity [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname/length initialization in entities.c and xmlstring.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlStrdup/xmlStrndup[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The harness in fuzz/xml.c that feeds input to xmlCtxtParseDocument: confirm that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39medge cases in entity definitions are handled or sanitized.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
